  3: "CHAT_CHANNEL_JOURNAL"
  3: "The Shadow Court began under the far more benign name of the Society for Unorthodox Magic. At the height of the Great Elven Empire, twelve powerful mages gathered in the capital city of Valen to push the boundaries of known magic and explore the unknown."
  3: "Some scholars claim their interests were unholy from the start, that the \'Society\' was merely a cover. Others believe they began with good intentions, but were corrupted by what they found."
  3: "One way or another, in their pursuit of greater magic, they made contact with the Shadow Realm, and the Dreadlord, who promised them immortality and power beyond their imagining, if they swore to serve him. And swear they did."
  3: "The Great War began in Valen, during the 875th year of the Skywarren Dynasty. Having pledged their service to the Dreadlord, the Shadow Court used their most powerful relic, the Onyx Shards, to open a portal in our reality... a portal through which the Dreadlord\'s armies swarmed through."
  3: "Valen fell instantly. Hundreds of thousands were killed, and centuries of art, knowledge, and culture were destroyed in a single day."
  3: "The elven civilization was entirely unprepared. After centuries of peace, they had set aside their armies and retired their battlemages. By the time they were able to marshal an opposition, half the continent had already fallen."
  3: "It was only through the courage and brilliance of two elves, the general Xaius and the battlemage Ellara, that the tide of battle turned. The two rallied the remaining cities and, with the help of the young races, fought the Court to a standstill."
  3: "The end of the Great War is history\'s greatest conundrum. In many ways this is the most important moment in the history of our world... and yet no record remains of how it happened."
  3: "What we know can be summed up on one parchment: the armies of the Court met the armies of the elves at the great ancient bastion of Cragheart. The Dreadlord himself was summoned, made flesh, and strode across the battlefields."
  3: "Yet when all was lost, the elven mages came together to perform one final ritual... a ritual that banished the Dreadlord and the Shadow Court and all their minions back to their realm."
  3: "A ritual that left every last elf gathered there dead as well."

  3: "Duke Erthax"

  3: "In life, Duke Erthax was known as Bastion of House Steelsorrow. A powerful battlemage, Bastion resented the peaceful era of the Skywarren Dynasty. He believed that the strongest should rule, and that the elves had allowed the weak to prosper instead."
  3: "Once turned to Shadow, Bastion became Duke Erthax. He was the vanguard of the Shadow\'s armies, a powerful warrior who always led the charge on the front lines."
  3: "Erthax relished combat and conquest, and fought with an unbridled bloodlust and skill. He was known to summon creatures of shadow, such as hounds and gargoyles, to fight at his side."
  3: "In life, Duchess Xenia was known as Eleryn of House Rosecoven. Renowned across the empire for her beauty and wit, Eleryn was often called the Rose of Valen, a pun on her family name."
  3: "In private circles, Eleryn had an entirely different reputation: that of a cruel, manipulative noblewoman, who relished in toying with the emotions of others, who smiled coldly as others dueled to the death in her name."
  3: "Corrupted by the Court, Eleryn became Duchess Xenia. A master of spycraft and intrigue, Xenia avoided the frontlines of battle. Instead, she worked behind the scenes, gathering intelligence, corrupting the weak, sowing chaos within the ranks of the elven armies."
  3: "Baron Vostrasz was known in life as Tameos of House Goldbearer. A powerful politician and merchant, Tameos was very influential in Valen, and responsible for the Society being founded in the first place."
  3: "There were other rumors about Tameos as well: of a taste for sadism, of dungeons hidden beneath his villa, of missing young women in his employ."
  3: "Once a member of the Court, Tameos became Baron Vostrasz. A cunning strategist, Vostrasz directed the Court\'s forces, and brokered alliances with those willing to side with the Shadows. He also serves as the Court\'s torturer. The less said of that, the better."
  3: "Read about..."
  3: "The Shadow Realm"
  3: "Creatures of Shadow"
  3: "The Realm\'s Corruption"
  3: "Back"
  3: "What do we know of the Shadow Realm? We know it is a world just like ours, a full reality. As two rooms in a house are separated, so our realm and the Shadow Realm sit side-by-side."
  3: "Some believe the Shadow Realm to be a dark mirror of our world, symmetrical but tainted, with each being here having an opposite there. Others believe it to be entirely different, perhaps unfathomably so."
  3: "The most we know is from the few who caught glimpses of it through portals and survived. Their accounts are of a hellish landscape, blighted by darkness, overrun ruins shrouded in death and horror."
  3: "The Shadow Realm teems with creatures of darkness, monstrous beasts that live seemingly only to slaughter and destroy."
  3: "Shadow Creatures take all forms: hounds and serpents, spiders ten feet tall, skeletal birds, and flame-breathing drakes."
  3: "The Shadow Creatures seem to exist at the service of the Shadow Court, fighting at the command of its members. Are they truly sentient and independent? Or are they merely weapons, deployed at the behest of their masters?"
  3: "Despite being sealed away, the Shadow Realm retains the ability to influence our world by entering the minds of the weak, the desperate, and the vulnerable."
  3: "Speaking to people through their dreams, through whispered voices at the back of their minds, the Shadow Court can corrupt elves, orcs, and humans, and seduce them into being agents of its agenda."
  3: "These agents are rumored to exist all over Morella, operating in shadow, working to undermine society and pave the way for the Court\'s return."
  3: "The Dreadlord is the monarch of the Shadow Realm. Very little is known about him: only that he is a creature of immense power and hunger, a terrifying force that controls all the Realm and its creatures."
  3: "Unlike the Shadow Court, who began life as elves in Morella, the Dreadlord has always existed in the Realm of Shadow. He was seen only once in our world, at the battle of Cragheart, when he took the form of a towering destructive colossus."
  3: "This mortal form was killed in the battle, its bones still resting there. Some believe the Dreadlord died with it. Others believe his essence still remains in the Shadow Court, reforming, perhaps seeking a new host."
